FROM issued_documents AS i
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i0.id, i0.approved_by, i0.archived_at, i0."CreatedAt", i0."DeletedAt", i0.doctor_name, i0.doctor_name_en, i0.document_body, i0.document_number, i0.is_deleted, i0.issued_at, i0.issued_by, i0.pdf_file_path, i0.qr_code_image_path, i0.qr_code_url, i0.qr_expires_at, i0.replacement_document_id, i0.request_id, i0.revocation_reason, i0.revoked_at, i0.revoked_by, i0.status, i0.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i0
    WHERE NOT (i0.is_deleted)
) AS i1 ON i.replacement_document_id = i1.id
WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted) AND i.id = @__id_0

FROM issued_documents AS i
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i0.id, i0.approved_by, i0.archived_at, i0."CreatedAt", i0."DeletedAt", i0.doctor_name, i0.doctor_name_en, i0.document_body, i0.document_number, i0.is_deleted, i0.issued_at, i0.issued_by, i0.pdf_file_path, i0.qr_code_image_path, i0.qr_code_url, i0.qr_expires_at, i0.replacement_document_id, i0.request_id, i0.revocation_reason, i0.revoked_at, i0.revoked_by, i0.status, i0.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i0
    WHERE NOT (i0.is_deleted)
) AS i1 ON i.replacement_document_id = i1.id
WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted) AND i.id = @__id_0
LIMIT 1

    WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted)
    ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS i0
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i0.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id

    FROM issued_documents AS i1
    WHERE NOT (i1.is_deleted)
) AS i2 ON i0.replacement_document_id = i2.id
ORDER BY i0.issued_at DESC

) AS i0
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i0.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i0.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i0.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i1.id, i1.approved_by, i1.archived_at, i1."CreatedAt", i1."DeletedAt", i1.doctor_name, i1.doctor_name_en, i1.document_body, i1.document_number, i1.is_deleted, i1.issued_at, i1.issued_by, i1.pdf_file_path, i1.qr_code_image_path, i1.qr_code_url, i1.qr_expires_at, i1.replacement_document_id, i1.request_id, i1.revocation_reason, i1.revoked_at, i1.revoked_by, i1.status, i1.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i1
    WHERE NOT (i1.is_deleted)
) AS i2 ON i0.replacement_document_id = i2.id
ORDER BY i0.issued_at DESC

FROM issued_documents AS i
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at

    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i0.id, i0.approved_by, i0.archived_at, i0."CreatedAt", i0."DeletedAt", i0.doctor_name, i0.doctor_name_en, i0.document_body, i0.document_number, i0.is_deleted, i0.issued_at, i0.issued_by, i0.pdf_file_path, i0.qr_code_image_path, i0.qr_code_url, i0.qr_expires_at, i0.replacement_document_id, i0.request_id, i0.revocation_reason, i0.revoked_at, i0.revoked_by, i0.status, i0.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i0
    WHERE NOT (i0.is_deleted)
) AS i1 ON i.replacement_document_id = i1.id
WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted) AND i.request_id = @__requestId_0
ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC

    ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS i0

    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at

SELECT i.id, i.approved_by, i.archived_at, i."CreatedAt", i."DeletedAt", i.doctor_name, i.doctor_name_en, i.document_body, i.document_number, i.is_deleted, i.issued_at, i.issued_by, i.pdf_file_path, i.qr_code_image_path, i.qr_code_url, i.qr_expires_at, i.replacement_document_id, i.request_id, i.revocation_reason, i.revoked_at, i.revoked_by, i.status, i.updated_at, d0.id, d0.assigned_to, d0.created_at, d0.created_by, d0."DeletedAt", d0.document_type_id, d0.is_deleted, d0.notes, d0.patient_name, d0.patient_name_en, d0.recipient_entity, d0.rejection_reason, d0.status, d0.updated_at, d1.id, d1.created_at, d1.description_ar, d1.description_en, d1.is_active, d1.name_ar, d1.name_en, d1.template_path, d1.updated_at, u.id, u.created_at, u.department, u.full_name, u.full_name_en, u.is_active, u.language_preference, u.password_hash, u.refresh_token, u.refresh_token_expiry, u.role, u.updated_at, u.username, u0.id, u0.created_at, u0.department, u0.full_name, u0.full_name_en, u0.is_active, u0.language_preference, u0.password_hash, u0.refresh_token, u0.refresh_token_expiry, u0.role, u0.updated_at, u0.username, u1.id, u1.created_at, u1.department, u1.full_name, u1.full_name_en, u1.is_active, u1.language_preference, u1.password_hash, u1.refresh_token, u1.refresh_token_expiry, u1.role, u1.updated_at, u1.username, i1.id, i1.approved_by, i1.archived_at, i1."CreatedAt", i1."DeletedAt", i1.doctor_name, i1.doctor_name_en, i1.document_body, i1.document_number, i1.is_deleted, i1.issued_at, i1.issued_by, i1.pdf_file_path, i1.qr_code_image_path, i1.qr_code_url, i1.qr_expires_at, i1.replacement_document_id, i1.request_id, i1.revocation_reason, i1.revoked_at, i1.revoked_by, i1.status, i1.updated_at
FROM issued_documents AS i
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i0.id, i0.approved_by, i0.archived_at, i0."CreatedAt", i0."DeletedAt", i0.doctor_name, i0.doctor_name_en, i0.document_body, i0.document_number, i0.is_deleted, i0.issued_at, i0.issued_by, i0.pdf_file_path, i0.qr_code_image_path, i0.qr_code_url, i0.qr_expires_at, i0.replacement_document_id, i0.request_id, i0.revocation_reason, i0.revoked_at, i0.revoked_by, i0.status, i0.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i0
    WHERE NOT (i0.is_deleted)
) AS i1 ON i.replacement_document_id = i1.id
WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted) AND i.request_id = @__requestId_0
ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC

SELECT i.id, i.approved_by, i.archived_at, i."CreatedAt", i."DeletedAt", i.doctor_name, i.doctor_name_en, i.document_body, i.document_number, i.is_deleted, i.issued_at, i.issued_by, i.pdf_file_path, i.qr_code_image_path, i.qr_code_url, i.qr_expires_at, i.replacement_document_id, i.request_id, i.revocation_reason, i.revoked_at, i.revoked_by, i.status, i.updated_at, d0.id, d0.assigned_to, d0.created_at, d0.created_by, d0."DeletedAt", d0.document_type_id, d0.is_deleted, d0.notes, d0.patient_name, d0.patient_name_en, d0.recipient_entity, d0.rejection_reason, d0.status, d0.updated_at, d1.id, d1.created_at, d1.description_ar, d1.description_en, d1.is_active, d1.name_ar, d1.name_en, d1.template_path, d1.updated_at, u.id, u.created_at, u.department, u.full_name, u.full_name_en, u.is_active, u.language_preference, u.password_hash, u.refresh_token, u.refresh_token_expiry, u.role, u.updated_at, u.username, u0.id, u0.created_at, u0.department, u0.full_name, u0.full_name_en, u0.is_active, u0.language_preference, u0.password_hash, u0.refresh_token, u0.refresh_token_expiry, u0.role, u0.updated_at, u0.username, u1.id, u1.created_at, u1.department, u1.full_name, u1.full_name_en, u1.is_active, u1.language_preference, u1.password_hash, u1.refresh_token, u1.refresh_token_expiry, u1.role, u1.updated_at, u1.username, i1.id, i1.approved_by, i1.archived_at, i1."CreatedAt", i1."DeletedAt", i1.doctor_name, i1.doctor_name_en, i1.document_body, i1.document_number, i1.is_deleted, i1.issued_at, i1.issued_by, i1.pdf_file_path, i1.qr_code_image_path, i1.qr_code_url, i1.qr_expires_at, i1.replacement_document_id, i1.request_id, i1.revocation_reason, i1.revoked_at, i1.revoked_by, i1.status, i1.updated_at
FROM issued_documents AS i
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT d.id, d.assigned_to, d.created_at, d.created_by, d."DeletedAt", d.document_type_id, d.is_deleted, d.notes, d.patient_name, d.patient_name_en, d.recipient_entity, d.rejection_reason, d.status, d.updated_at
    FROM document_requests AS d
    WHERE NOT (d.is_deleted)
) AS d0 ON i.request_id = d0.id
INNER JOIN document_types AS d1 ON d0.document_type_id = d1.id
INNER JOIN users AS u ON d0.created_by = u.id
INNER JOIN users AS u0 ON i.issued_by = u0.id
LEFT JOIN users AS u1 ON i.revoked_by = u1.id
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT i0.id, i0.approved_by, i0.archived_at, i0."CreatedAt", i0."DeletedAt", i0.doctor_name, i0.doctor_name_en, i0.document_body, i0.document_number, i0.is_deleted, i0.issued_at, i0.issued_by, i0.pdf_file_path, i0.qr_code_image_path, i0.qr_code_url, i0.qr_expires_at, i0.replacement_document_id, i0.request_id, i0.revocation_reason, i0.revoked_at, i0.revoked_by, i0.status, i0.updated_at
    FROM issued_documents AS i0
    WHERE NOT (i0.is_deleted)
) AS i1 ON i.replacement_document_id = i1.id
WHERE NOT (i.is_deleted) AND i.request_id = @__requestId_0
ORDER BY i.issued_at DESC
